CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));

CREATE TABLE PlayerGameHistory (PlayerID INT, GameID INT, PlayTimeInHours INT, Score INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID), FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID));</t><stat>insert into playergamehistory (playerid, gameid, playtimeinhours, score) values (1, 1, 10, 500);</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE GameReview (ReviewID INT PRIMARY KEY, GameID INT, PlayerID INT, Rating INT, ReviewText TEXT, FOREIGN KEY (GameID) REFERENCES Game(GameID), FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));

CREATE TABLE PlayerInventory (InventoryID INT PRIMARY KEY, PlayerID INT, ItemName VARCHAR(50), Quantity INT, FOREIGN KEY (PlayerID) REFERENCES Player(PlayerID));
